double protectionLegFull = (1d - recoveryRate) *\n        underlyingPricer.protectionFull(underlyingCds, rates.getFirst(), rates.getSecond(),\n            referenceDate, effectiveStartDate);\n\n    // For a tranche, we scale the protection leg by the spread of the tranche\n    // This represents the expected loss between attachment and detachment points\n    double trancheSpread = cdsTranche.getDetachmentPoint() - cdsTranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    double protectionLeg = protectionLegFull * trancheSpread;\n\n    // Compute risky annuity (RPV01)\n    double rpv01 = underlyingPricer.riskyAnnuity(\n        underlyingCds, rates.getFirst(), rates.getSecond(),\n        referenceDate, stepinDate, effectiveStartDate, priceType);\n\n    // Scale notional to reflect the tranche size\n    double notional = cdsTranche.getNotional();\n    double amount = cdsTranche.getBuySell().normalize(notional) * rates.getThird() *\n        (protectionLeg - rpv01 * cdsTranche.getFixedRate());\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(cdsTranche.getCurrency(), amount);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value sensitivity of the product.\n   * <p>\n   * The present value sensitivity of the product is the sensitivity of the present value to the underlying curves.\n   *\n   * @param cdsTranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder presentValueSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    if (isExpired(cdsTranche, ratesProvider)) {\n      return PointSensitivityBuilder.none();\n    }\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n    return underlyingPricer.presentValueSensitivity(underlyingCds, ratesProvider, referenceDate, refData);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private boolean isExpired(ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche, CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider) {\n    return ratesProvider.getValuationDate().isAfter(cdsTranche.getProtectionEndDate());\n  }\n\n  private Triple<CreditDiscountFactors, LegalEntitySurvivalProbabilities, Double> reduceDiscountFactors(\n      ResolvedCds cds,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider) {\n    return underlyingPricer.reduceDiscountFactors(cds, ratesProvider);\n  }\n\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Wraps CdsTranche with TradeInfo and optional upfront fee\n// - Implements ProductTrade and ResolvableTrade interfaces\n// - summarize() method: formats tranche details (attachment%-detachment%)\n// - Wraps ResolvedCdsTranche with TradeInfo\n// - Holds settlement payment information\n// - Input to pricer functions\n// - Default TradeInfo.empty() if not provided\n```\n\n**File path**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java`\n\n### modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java\n\n```java\n// Created new file implementing ISDA tranche pricer\n// Key components:\n// - Implements CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade>\n// - Registers supported measures in CALCULATORS map:\n//   - PRESENT_VALUE, UNIT_PRICE, PRINCIPAL\n//   - IR01_CALIBRATED_PARALLEL, PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM\n// - requirements() method: specifies CreditRatesMarketDataLookup needed\n// - calculate() method: orchestrates measure calculations\n// - Uses CdsTranchesMeasureCalculations for actual computations\n```\n\n**File path**: `/workspace/modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java`\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe CDS Tranche implementation follows OpenGamma Strata's established patterns:\n\n1. **Product Hierarchy**: CdsTranche extends CdsIndex concept by adding attachment/detachment points that define the subordination level. The tranche represents credit risk between these loss thresholds.\n\n2. **Joda-Beans Pattern**: All product classes use `@BeanDefinition` annotation with `@PropertyDefinition` fields, enabling immutable beans with builder pattern. This provides automatic serialization, equals/hashCode, and metadata generation.\n\n3. **Resolve Pattern**: Products implement `Resolvable<T>` to expand from abstract contracts (with calendars, schedules) to concrete resolved forms with explicit cash flow dates. For tranches:\n   - `CdsTranche.resolve()` → `ResolvedCdsTranche`\n   - `CdsTrancheTrade.resolve()` → `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade`\n\n4. **Notional Scaling**: Key insight - tranche notional is scaled by the spread between attachment and detachment points:\n   ```\n   trancheNotional = underlyingIndex.notional * (detachmentPoint - attachmentPoint)\n   ```\n   This ensures the tranche value is proportional to its slice of the index.\n\n5. **Pricing Logic**: The `IsdaCdsTranchePricer` extracts the underlying CDS index and:\n   - Computes protection leg for full portfolio\n   - Scales by tranche spread to get tranche protection value\n   - Uses standard annuity calculations (RPV01) for premium leg\n   - Final PV = tranche_notional * (protection_leg - rpv01 * coupon_rate)\n\n6. **Calculation Integration**: The `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction` integrates with Strata's scenario engine:\n   - Specifies required market data (CreditRatesProvider with index curves)\n   - Supports multi-scenario calculations via `CreditRatesScenarioMarketData`\n   - Maps measures to calculation methods\n   - Returns results for each scenario in arrays\n\n### Design Decisions\n\n1. **Underlying Index Reference**: `CdsTranche` holds a `CdsIndex` reference rather than individual fields. This allows reuse of index construction logic and ensures consistency.\n\n2. **Point Validation**: Attachment and detachment points must satisfy:\n   - Both in (0, 1) exclusive range to represent loss percentages\n   - attachment < detachment\n   - Validation occurs in `@ImmutablePreBuild` method\n\n3. **Payment Period Scaling**: Rather than duplicating CreditCouponPaymentPeriod logic, we scale existing periods from the resolved index by adjusting notional. This maintains consistency in day count, accrual dates, etc.\n\n4. **Pricer Composition**: `IsdaCdsTranchePricer` reuses `IsdaCdsProductPricer` for core calculations. This minimizes duplication and ensures consistent treatment of:\n   - Accrual-on-default formulas\n   - Recovery rates\n   - Discount factors and survival probabilities\n\n5. **Measure Calculations**: Following `CdsIndexMeasureCalculations` pattern, single-scenario and multi-scenario methods are separated. This allows flexible scenario handling while keeping calculation logic centralized.\n\n### Architecture Benefits\n\n1. **Type Safety**: Immutable beans with Joda-Beans prevent accidental modification after creation\n2. **Serialization**: Automatic serialization support for persistence/distribution\n3. **Introspection**: Metadata access through MetaProperty enables generic tools\n4. **Builder Pattern**: Fluent API for construction without reflection\n5. **Consistency**: Following existing patterns reduces learning curve and maintenance burden\n\n### Compilation Status\n\nThe implementation is structured but requires verification of:\n- Joda-Bean property definitions and hashCode generation\n- Proper builder implementation details\n- Compatibility with existing CDS infrastructure\n\nAll core files have been created with correct interfaces and method signatures matching the CdsIndex pattern.\n\n## Files Created\n\n1. index credit curve as well as\n * the information on the relevant recovery rate and index factor.\n * <p>\n * This pricer invokes the implementation in {@link IsdaCdsProductPricer}.\n */\npublic class /**\n   * The pricer for single name CDS.\n   */\n  private final IsdaCdsProductPricer underlyingPricer;\n\n  /**\n   * Constructor specifying the formula to use for the accrued on default calculation.\n   *\n   * @param formula  the formula\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer(AccrualOnDefaultFormula formula) {\n    this.underlyingPricer = new IsdaCdsProductPricer(formula);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Gets the accrual-on-default formula used in this pricer.\n   *\n   * @return the formula\n   */\n  public AccrualOnDefaultFormula getAccrualOnDefaultFormula() {\n    return underlyingPricer.getAccrualOnDefaultFormula();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price of the CDS tranche product, which is the minus of the present value per unit notional.\n   * <p>\n   * This method can calculate the clean or dirty price, see {@link PriceType}.\n   * If calculating the clean price, the accrued interest is calculated based on the step-in date.\n   *\n   * @param cdsTranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the price\n   */\n  public double price(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n    return underlyingPricer.price(underlyingCds, ratesProvider, referenceDate, priceType, refData);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price sensitivity of the product.\n   * <p>\n   * The price sensitivity of the product is the sensitivity of price to the underlying curves.\n   *\n   * @param cdsTranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder priceSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n    return underlyingPricer.priceSensitivity(underlyingCds, ratesProvider, referenceDate, refData);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche product.\n   * <p>\n   * The present value of the product is based on {@code referenceDate}.\n   * This is typically the valuation date, or cash settlement date if the product is associated with a {@code Trade}.\n   * <p>\n   * This method can calculate the clean or dirty present value, see {@link PriceType}.\n   * If calculating the clean value, the accrued interest is calculated based on the step-in date.\n   *\n   * @param cdsTranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    if (isExpired(cdsTranche, ratesProvider)) {\n      return CurrencyAmount.of(cdsTranche.getCurrency(), 0d);\n    }\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n    LocalDate stepinDate = cdsTranche.getStepinDateOffset().adjust(ratesProvider.getValuationDate(), refData);\n    LocalDate effectiveStartDate = underlyingCds.calculateEffectiveStartDate(stepinDate);\n    double recoveryRate = underlyingPricer.recoveryRate(underlyingCds, ratesProvider);\n    Triple<CreditDiscountFactors, LegalEntitySurvivalProbabilities, Double> rates =\n        reduceDiscountFactors(underlyingCds, ratesProvider);\n\n    // Compute protection leg for the full CDS\n    double protectionLegFull = (1d - recoveryRate) *\n        underlyingPricer.protectionFull(underlyingCds, rates.getFirst(), rates.getSecond(),\n            referenceDate, effectiveStartDate);\n\n    // For a tranche, we scale the protection leg by the spread of the tranche\n    // This represents the expected loss between attachment and detachment points\n    double trancheSpread = cdsTranche.getDetachmentPoint() - cdsTranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    double protectionLeg = protectionLegFull * trancheSpread;\n\n    // Compute risky annuity (RPV01)\n    double rpv01 = underlyingPricer.riskyAnnuity(\n        underlyingCds, rates.getFirst(), rates.getSecond(),\n        referenceDate, stepinDate, effectiveStartDate, priceType);\n\n    // Scale notional to reflect the tranche size\n    double notional = cdsTranche.getNotional();\n    double amount = cdsTranche.getBuySell().normalize(notional) * rates.getThird() *\n        (protectionLeg - rpv01 * cdsTranche.getFixedRate());\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(cdsTranche.getCurrency(), amount);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value sensitivity of the product.\n   * <p>\n   * The present value sensitivity of the product is the sensitivity of the present value to the underlying curves.\n   *\n   * @param cdsTranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder presentValueSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    if (isExpired(cdsTranche, ratesProvider)) {\n      return PointSensitivityBuilder.none();\n    }\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n    return underlyingPricer.presentValueSensitivity(underlyingCds, ratesProvider, referenceDate, refData);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private boolean isExpired(ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche, CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider) {\n    return ratesProvider.getValuationDate().isAfter(cdsTranche.getProtectionEndDate());\n  }\n\n  private Triple<CreditDiscountFactors, LegalEntitySurvivalProbabilities, Double> reduceDiscountFactors(\n      ResolvedCds cds,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider) {\n    return underlyingPricer.reduceDiscountFactors(cds, ratesProvider);\n priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n    return underlyingPricer.price(underlyingCds, ratesProvider, referenceDate, priceType, refData);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price sensitivity of the product.\n   * <p>\n   * The price sensitivity of the product is the sensitivity of price to the * @return the present value sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder priceSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n    return underlyingPricer.priceSensitivity(underlyingCds, ratesProvider, referenceDate, refData);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche product.\n   * <p>\n   * The present value of the product is based on {@code referenceDate}.\n   * This is typically the valuation date, or cash settlement date if the product is associated with a {@code Trade}.\n   * <p>\n   * This method can calculate the clean or dirty present value, see {@link PriceType}.\n   * If calculating the clean value, the accrued interest is calculated based on the step-in date.\n   *\n   * @param cdsTranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    if (isExpired(cdsTranche, ratesProvider)) {\n      return CurrencyAmount.of(cdsTranche.getCurrency(), 0d);\n    }\n    // Use the underlying index's toSingleNameCds() to get equivalent single-name CDS\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n\n    // Scale the notional by the tranche spread to get tranche-specific value\n    double trancheSpread = cdsTranche.getDetachmentPoint() - cdsTranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n\n    // Get the PV of the equivalent single-name CDS\n attachment/detachment points\n    double scaledAmount = cdsValue.getAmount() * trancheSpread;\n\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(cdsTranche.getCurrency(), scaledAmount);\n  }\n\n reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder presentValueSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    if (isExpired(cdsTranche, ratesProvider)) {\n      return PointSensitivityBuilder.none();\n    }\n    ResolvedCds underlyingCds = cdsTranche.getUnderlyingIndex().toSingleNameCds();\n    return underlyingPricer.presentValueSensitivity(underlyingCds, ratesProvider, referenceDate, refData);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private boolean isExpired(ResolvedCdsTranche cdsTranche, CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider) {\n    return ratesProvider.getValuationDate().isAfter(cdsTranche.getProtectionEndDate());\n  }\n\n  private Triple<CreditDiscountFactors, The tranche represents credit risk between these loss thresholds.\n\n2. **Joda-Beans Pattern**: All product classes use `@BeanDefinition` annotation with `@PropertyDefinition` fields, enabling immutable beans with builder pattern. This provides automatic serialization, equals/hashCode, and metadata generation.\n\n3. **Resolve Pattern**: Products implement `Resolvable<T>` to expand from abstract contracts (with calendars, schedules) to concrete resolved forms with explicit cash flow dates. For tranches:\n   - `CdsTranche.resolve()` → `ResolvedCdsTranche`\n   - `CdsTrancheTrade.resolve()` → `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade`\n\n4. **Notional Scaling**: Key insight - tranche notional is scaled by the spread between attachment and detachment points:\n   ```\n   trancheNotional = underlyingIndex.notional * (detachmentPoint - attachmentPoint)\n   ```\n   This ensures the tranche value is proportional to its slice of the index.\n\n5. **Pricing Logic**: The `IsdaCdsTranchePricer` extracts the underlying CDS index and:\n   - Computes protection leg for full portfolio\n   - Scales by tranche spread to get tranche protection value\n   - Uses standard annuity calculations (RPV01) for premium leg\n   - Final PV = tranche_notional * (protection_leg - rpv01 * coupon_rate)\n\n6. **Calculation Integration**: The `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction` integrates with Strata's scenario engine:\n   - Specifies required market data (CreditRatesProvider with index curves)\n   - Supports multi-scenario calculations via `CreditRatesScenarioMarketData`\n   - Maps measures to calculation methods\n   - Returns results for each scenario in arrays\n\n### Design Decisions\n\n1. **Underlying Index Reference**: `CdsTranche` holds a `CdsIndex` reference rather than individual fields. This allows reuse of index construction logic and ensures consistency.\n\n2. **Point Validation**: Attachment and detachment points must satisfy:\n   - Both in (0, 1) exclusive range to represent loss percentages\n   - attachment < detachment\n   - Validation occurs in `@ImmutablePreBuild` method\n\n3. **Payment Period Scaling**: Rather than duplicating CreditCouponPaymentPeriod logic, we scale existing periods from the resolved index by adjusting notional. This maintains consistency in day count, accrual dates, etc.\n\n4. **Pricer Composition**: `IsdaCdsTranchePricer` reuses `IsdaCdsProductPricer` for core calculations. This minimizes duplication and ensures consistent treatment of:\n   - Accrual-on-default formulas\n   - Recovery rates\n   - Discount factors and survival probabilities\n\n5. **Measure Calculations**: Following `CdsIndexMeasureCalculations` pattern, single-scenario and multi-scenario methods are separated. This allows flexible scenario handling while keeping calculation logic centralized.\n\n### Architecture Benefits\n\n1. **Type Safety**: Immutable beans with Joda-Beans prevent accidental modification after creation\n2. **Serialization**: Automatic serialization support for persistence/distribution\n3. **Introspection**: Metadata access through MetaProperty enables generic tools\n4. **Builder Pattern**: Fluent API for construction without reflection\n5. **Consistency**: Following existing patterns reduces learning curve and maintenance burden\n\n### Compilation Status\n\nThe implementation
